
% Default to the notebook output style

    


% Inherit from the specified cell style.




    
\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    

    
    
    % Colors for the hyperref package
    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}

    \subsubsection{Import Data Sets (includes data cleaning and seperating
data into training and testing
sets)}\label{import-data-sets-includes-data-cleaning-and-seperating-data-into-training-and-testing-sets}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}2}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}income dataset (by default, is already split into test and train data)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}title headers for the dataset}
        \PY{n}{income\PYZus{}header} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{age}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{workclass}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{fnlwgt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{education}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{education\PYZhy{}num}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{marital\PYZhy{}status}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{occupation}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relationship}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PYZbs{}

        \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}Income} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{income\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{15000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Last column: Labels (0 or 1)}
        \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}Poker\PYZus{}1\PYZus{}Cards} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{poker\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{15000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{]}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predict with knowledge of 1 card}
        \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}Poker\PYZus{}2\PYZus{}Cards} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{poker\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{15000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{7}\PY{p}{]}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predict with knowledge of 2 cards}
        \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}Poker\PYZus{}3\PYZus{}Cards} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{poker\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{15000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{]}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predict with knowledge of 3 cards}
        \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}Poker\PYZus{}4\PYZus{}Cards} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{poker\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{15000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predict with knowledge of 4 cards}
        \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}Poker\PYZus{}5\PYZus{}Cards} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{poker\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{15000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predict with knowledge of 5 cards}
        \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}Poker} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{poker\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{15000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]} 
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}get all the data}

    \subsubsection{Classifier 2: SVM Using Linear
Kernel}\label{classifier-2-svm-using-linear-kernel}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}33}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}svm with cross validation of 3}
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{svm}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,}\PYZbs{}
                        \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Initialize model.}
             \PY{n}{svm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{SVC}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{kernel}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{linear}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \paragraph{Since SVM was taking more than hours to run just one split, I
decided to take out the SVM model on the poker
dataset}\label{since-svm-was-taking-more-than-hours-to-run-just-one-split-i-decided-to-take-out-the-svm-model-on-the-poker-dataset}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Y\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}MLP = poker\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}df.iloc[:15000, \PYZhy{}1] }
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} X\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}MLP = poker\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}df.iloc[0:, 0:\PYZhy{}1]  }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Y\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}MLP = poker\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}df.iloc[0:, \PYZhy{}1] }

         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Y\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}MLP = Y\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}MLP.apply(lambda i: \PYZhy{}1 if i \PYZlt{}1 else 1)}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} scaler = StandardScaler()}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} scaler.fit(X\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}MLP) }
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} X\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}MLP = scaler.transform(X\PYZus{}poker\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}MLP)}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}57}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZsh{}courtesey of https://github.com/aditisrinivas97/Pokerman}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} def svm\PYZus{}poker(X\PYZus{}train, Y\PYZus{}train, X\PYZus{}test, Y\PYZus{}test):}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     \PYZsh{} Store the accuracies}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     accuracy = list()}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     \PYZsh{} Store the predictions}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     predictions = list()}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     for trial in range(5):}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         classifier = SVC(kernel=\PYZsq{}linear\PYZsq{})}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         result = classifier.fit(X\PYZus{}train, Y\PYZus{}train)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         prediction = classifier.predict(X\PYZus{}test)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         predictions.append(prediction)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         curr\PYZus{}accuracy = accuracy\PYZus{}score(Y\PYZus{}test, prediction)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         accuracy.append(curr\PYZus{}accuracy)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     print(accuracy)}
             
             
\end{Verbatim}

    \subsubsection{Classifier 4: Multi-layer
Perceptron}\label{classifier-4-multi-layer-perceptron}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}86}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}multi layer perceptron with cross validation of 3}
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{mlp}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,}\PYZbs{}
                        \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Initialize model.}
             \PY{n}{mlp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{MLPClassifier}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{learning\PYZus{}rate\PYZus{}init} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.02}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}iter} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{2000}\PY{p}{)}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}102}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZsh{}courtesey of https://github.com/aditisrinivas97/Pokerman}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} def mlp\PYZus{}poker(X\PYZus{}train, Y\PYZus{}train, X\PYZus{}test, Y\PYZus{}test):}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     \PYZsh{} Store the accuracies}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     accuracy = list()}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     \PYZsh{} Store the predictions}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     predictions = list()}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     for trial in range(5):}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         classifier = MLPClassifier(activation = \PYZsq{}tanh\PYZsq{}, learning\PYZus{}rate\PYZus{}init = 0.02, max\PYZus{}iter = 2000, random\PYZus{}state = trial)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         result = classifier.fit(X\PYZus{}train, Y\PYZus{}train)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         prediction = classifier.predict(X\PYZus{}test)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         predictions.append(prediction)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         curr\PYZus{}accuracy = accuracy\PYZus{}score(Y\PYZus{}test, prediction)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}         accuracy.append(curr\PYZus{}accuracy)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     print(accuracy)}
              
              
\end{Verbatim}

    \subsubsection{Classifier 5: Decision
Tree}\label{classifier-5-decision-tree}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}104}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}decision tree with cross validation of 3}
          \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{tree}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,}\PYZbs{}
                         \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{title3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Initialize model.}
